						remove_ideas = RAJ_marginalized_muslim_community
						remove_ideas = RAJ_marginalized_muslim_community_angry
						add_ideas = RAJ_marginalized_muslim_community_happy
					}
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ENG
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = CAN
							tag = SAF
							tag = RAJ
							tag = AST
							tag = NZL
							tag = NFL
							tag = MAL
						}
					}
					OR = {
						has_government = ROOT
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
					}
					random = {
						chance = 50
						every_enemy_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war_with = PREV
							}
							white_peace = PREV
						}
						leave_faction = yes
						set_country_flag = ENG_decolonization_left_faction

							type = alliance
							id = "ENG"

						}
					}
				}
			}

				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ENG
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = CAN
							tag = SAF
							tag = RAJ
							tag = AST
							tag = NZL
							tag = NFL
							tag = MAL
						}
					}

						}

					}

			if = {
				limit = {

					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = SAF }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RAJ }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AST }

				}

							has_war_together_with = ENG

						}
					}

				}

					limit = {
						NOT = {
							CAN = {
								has_war_together_with = ENG
								has_country_flag = ENG_decolonization_left_faction
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							AST = {
								has_war_together_with = ENG

								has_war_together_with = ENG

						}

									tag = AST

		}

			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = ENG4_modern_tanks }
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = ENG4_human_wave_doctrine
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_1
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = ENG4_establish_high_command
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_2
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = ENG4_never_ending_barrage
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_3
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = ENG4_blitzkrieg
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_4
			}
			else = {
			    custom_effect_tooltip = RI_mobile_tactics
			}
		}
	}

		focus = {
		id = ENG4_more_factories
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_mil_factory
		x = 80
		y = 5
		cost = 10

		prerequisite = { focus = ENG4_night_vision }
    	prerequisite = { focus = ENG4_peoples_storm
                         focus = ENG4_peoples_officers }
		prerequisite = { focus = ENG4_combined_arms }
		
		completion_reward = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = arms_factory
										size > 0
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

		focus = {
		id = ENG4_dockyards
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_naval_dockyard
		x = 96
		y = 3
		cost = 10

		prerequisite = { focus = ENG4_modern_pirates
						 focus = ENG4_old_tactics }
		

		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							dockyard > 0
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 2
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_coastal = yes
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = naval_effort_built }
					any_owned_state = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
		}
